 2334 |  3  Checkerboard.s      2 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * Ported from FTA's ESSAI2.S (1989) for Merlin32
 2335 |  3  Checkerboard.s      3 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | *
 2336 |  3  Checkerboard.s      4 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * Pre-computes 8 frames of perspective-correct checkerboard
 2337 |  3  Checkerboard.s      5 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * into IMAGE buffer ($030000). Each frame is offset by a
 2338 |  3  Checkerboard.s      6 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * different horizontal scroll amount.
 2339 |  3  Checkerboard.s      7 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | *
 2340 |  3  Checkerboard.s      8 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * Uses colors $4 and $E for the two stripe colors.
 2341 |  3  Checkerboard.s      9 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * At runtime, palette swapping between palette 0/2 on
 2342 |  3  Checkerboard.s     10 | Comment     | 00 |         |    0 | 00/0F18               | * alternating scanlines creates the full checkerboard effect.
